in the ruins chapter amara hadnt seen the count of calderon for months when she and her escort of knights aeris swept down into the calderon valley and to bernards fortresstown of garrison she felt a the people moving around the improvised market were marat the pale barbarians and their beasts had been little but an infrequent and vicious menace from the perspective of aleran history and only manacles strangled by one of his own chains the elderly high lord cereus ventis though the legal master of the city did not command the respect of the vigilantes or their supporters nor possess the that made the walls tremble beneath his boots the sound loud enough to drown even the howling chaos of the battle for a moment the ram had reached the gate and it seemed inconceivable that it could the slavers option provide the inverse of that sensation and just as intensely discipline collars were sometimes used to restrain particularly dangerous furycrafters being held for trial in the legal system though such cases were historically rare but in the past century or so their manufacture and use had become far more widespread as the institution of slavery deepened and darkened prolonged exposure to the collars could shatter the mind and will continually forced through agonies of torment and euphoria victims were compelled to obey the slaver and forced to experience pleasure as they did so over time often years many such slaves were reduced to little more than animals their humanity torn from them and replaced with the simple irresistible compulsion of the collar chillingly they
